GT Equivalence Verification (PO42)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - c1*beta*v
Candidate formulas: 107

GT (fixed):
\[
-0.0313132230839372\,v^3\;-\;0.657729448450456\,v\sin(x)\;-\;1.31545889690091\,v\;+\;0.383670562566156\,\sin(t)
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **exactly** these four terms and **no others**:
1) a pure \(v^3\) term,  
2) a \(v\sin(x)\) term (note: depends on \(\sin(x)\), not polynomial in \(x\), not \(v x\), not \(v|x|\), etc.),  
3) a pure \(v\) term,  
4) a pure \(\sin(t)\) term (can be written as \(\cos(t+\phi)\) via phase shift).

Also, GT has **no** constant offset, no \(v x\), no \(v x^2\), no \(v/x^{1/3}\), no exponentials/logs, no \(v^5\), etc. Such extra structures must be removable by setting their coefficients to 0. But crucially: the candidate must still be able to produce the \(v\sin(x)\) term; if it cannot, it can’t match.

Now check candidates (grouping repeated structure; whenever a candidate only has polynomial-in-\(x\) couplings like \(v x\) or \(v x^2\), it cannot equal \(v\sin(x)\) for all real \(x\)).

---

### Candidates 1–3
They have \(c7 v x\), \(c1 v x^2\), \(c8 v/x^{1/3}\), optional constant/exp. None has \(v\sin(x)\).
- You can zero out unwanted terms, and use \(c3\cos(c4+t)\) to match \(\sin(t)\) (phase shift works), and \(c2 v^3\) + \(c0 v\) to match the \(v^3\) and \(v\) terms.
- But there is **no way** to create \(-0.6577\,v\sin(x)\).
So 1–3: **no match**.

### Candidates 4–5
Have \(v^3\), \(v\), \(\cos(t+\phi)\), plus \(v x\), \(v x^2\), \(v/x^{1/3}\), and an extra \(x\sin(\cdot)\) or \(x\cos(\cdot)\) term.
- Still no \(v\sin(x)\).
So 4–5: **no match**.

### Candidate 6
Adds \(v^5\) and \(v\log(c9|x|+1)\). Still no \(v\sin(x)\). Also \(|x|\) is not equivalent to \(x\) globally.
So 6: **no match**.

### Candidates 7–9
They include \(\sin(c3 t+c4)\) or \(\cos(t+\phi)\) and \(v^3\), but \(x\)-dependence is via \(v x\), \(v x^2\), \(v/x^{1/3}\), or \(t^{c4}\), not \(v\sin(x)\).
So 7–9: **no match**.

### Candidates 10–13
Contain \(v^5\), exponentials, logs, \(|v|\), etc. None contains \(\sin(x)\) multiplied by \(v\).
So 10–13: **no match**.

### Candidate 14
Has rational terms \(v/(c7 x+c8)\) and \(1/(c7 x+c8)\), but not \(v\sin(x)\).
So 14: **no match**.

### Candidates 15–22
Various mixes: some have \(\cos(t+\phi)\), \(v^3\), but \(x\)-dependence is \(v x\), \(v x^2\), \(v/x^{1/3}\), logs, \(v|v|\), \(v\cos(\cdot)\), powers \((t+c)^p\). None has \(v\sin(x)\).
So 15–22: **no match**.

### Candidates 23–28
Include \(\cos(t+\phi)\), \(v^3\), maybe \(v^5\), \(\exp(c x)\), etc. Still no \(v\sin(x)\).
So 23–28: **no match**.

### Candidates 29–35
Again polynomial \(x\) couplings and extra nonlinearities (duplicate \(v^3\), \(v^5\), logs, exp in \(v\), linear \(t\) terms). No \(v\sin(x)\).
So 29–35: **no match**.

### Candidates 36–43
Contain extra \(t(x+c)^p\), \(t(v+c)^p\), rational \(x/(c x^2+1)\), linear \(x\), constants, \(v^5\). No \(v\sin(x)\).
So 36–43: **no match**.

### Candidates 44–48
Have \(\exp(c x)\), \(v^5\), constants, \(x^3\). No \(v\sin(x)\).
So 44–48: **no match**.

### Candidates 49–53
Have \(\sin(c3 v+c4)\) or \(\exp(c v)\) or \(t^{c4}\), plus \(\cos(t+\phi)\). No \(v\sin(x)\).
So 49–53: **no match**.

### Candidates 54–60
Some include \(v\log(|x|+1)\) or \(v(x+c)^p\). Still no \(v\sin(x)\).
So 54–60: **no match**.

### Candidate 61
Has \(v|x|\) (not \(v\sin(x)\), and abs is not removable into sine). No match.

### Candidate 62
Has \(v x^{c7}\) (power law), not \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 63–64
Have \(v\log(|x|+1)\) and possibly \(v x\). Not \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidate 65
Has \(\sin(c3 x+c4)\) **but it is not multiplied by \(v\)**; GT needs \(v\sin(x)\). You cannot multiply by \(v\) via parameter choice. So no match.

### Candidates 66–70
Contain \(\log(c v+1)\) or \(v x\) etc. No \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 71–73
Have \(x\cos(c8 x+c9)\) or \(\cos(c8|x|+1)\) or \(x^{c8}\log(|v|+1)\). None equals \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 74–81
Include constants, \(t\), \(x\), \(\log(c x+1)\), etc. No \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidate 82
Has \(v\sin(c8 t+c9)\): sine depends on \(t\), not \(x\). GT needs \(v\sin(x)\) and separately \(\sin(t)\) without \(v\). No match.

### Candidate 83
Has \(\cos(c8\exp(c9 x^2))\): wrong functional form. No match.

### Candidates 84–89
Add \(x^3\), \(x^5\), constants, \(|v|\), rational \(x/(c x^2+1)\), \(\log(c x+1)\). No \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidate 90
Has \(\log(c|x|+1)\) (not multiplied by \(v\sin\)). No match.

### Candidates 91, 103
Use \(\max(0,x)^{p}\): piecewise, not \(\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 92–97
Have \(x^{c4}\), \(\exp(c x)\), linear \(x\), constants. No \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 98–102
Polynomial couplings and constants; no \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidate 104
Has \(x^3\) term; no \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

### Candidates 105–107
Have \(\log(c t+1)\) or \(t^{c4}\) etc. No \(v\sin(x)\). No match.

---

### Trig phase-shift check (where relevant)
Many candidates have \(c\cos(c'+t)\), which *can* match \(0.38367056\sin(t)\) by choosing:
- amplitude \(c = 0.383670562566156\)
- phase \(c' = \pi/2\) (since \(\cos(t+\pi/2)=-\sin t\); use \(-\pi/2\) to get \(+\sin t\), adjusting sign via amplitude).
So the \(\sin(t)\) part is not the blocker.

### The blocker for all candidates
None of the 107 candidates contains a term of the form \(v\sin(x)\) (with sine depending on \(x\) and multiplied by \(v\)). The closest is candidate 65’s \(\sin(c3 x+c4)\) but it is **not multiplied by \(v\)**, and candidate 82’s \(v\sin(\cdot)\) depends on \(t\), not \(x\). Therefore no parameter choice can make any candidate equal the GT for all real \(x,t,v\).

GT Equivalence Verification (PO42)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*sin(x)*v - c1*beta*v
Candidates evaluated: 107
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `-0.0313*v³ - 0.6577*v*sin(x) - 1.3155*v + 0.3837*sin(t)`

The key terms are:
1. `v³` term
2. `v*sin(x)` term
3. `v` term (linear)
4. `sin(t)` term

The critical question is whether any candidate's basis functions can represent `v*sin(x)`. The GT has `sin(x)` multiplied by `v`, which is a specific transcendental function of `x`.

All candidates use combinations of terms like `v*x²`, `v*x`, `v/x^(1/3)`, `v*log(|x|+1)`, `cos(t+c)`, `v³`, `v⁵`, etc.

**Key analysis:** Can `v*sin(x)` be represented by combinations of `v*x²`, `v*x`, `v/x^(1/3)`, and similar terms?

`sin(x)` is a transcendental function. It cannot be exactly represented by any finite combination of polynomial terms (`x`, `x²`, `x^(-1/3)`) and `log` terms. These are linearly independent basis functions. So we need a candidate that explicitly contains `v*sin(x)` or an equivalent.

Let me check if any candidate has `sin(x)` or similar:

- **Candidate 49:** has `sin(c3*v + c4)` — this is sin of v, not sin of x
- **Candidate 65:** has `sin(c3*x + c4)` — this is `sin(c3*x + c4)` which, when multiplied... wait, it's `c2*sin(c3*x + c4)`, not `v*sin(x)`. This is just `sin` of x without the `v` multiplier. So it can't match `v*sin(x)`.
- **Candidate 71:** has `x*cos(c8*x + c9)` — not `v*sin(x)`

None of the candidates contain a `v*sin(x)` term. The candidates all try to approximate `v*sin(x)` using polynomial-like terms in x (like `v*x`, `v*x²`, `v/x^(1/3)`, `v*log(|x|+1)`), but these can never exactly equal `v*sin(x)` for all x.

Since `sin(x)` is transcendental and linearly independent from all polynomial, power-law, and logarithmic functions, **no finite combination of these basis functions can exactly reproduce `sin(x)`**.

Therefore, **none of the candidates** can be made exactly equivalent to the GT.

Let me do a final sweep to make sure I haven't missed any candidate with `v*sin(x)`:
- Candidates with `sin`: 7 (sin(c3*t+c4)), 49 (sin(c3*v+c4)), 65 (c2*sin(c3*x+c4)), 82 (v*sin(c8*t+c9)), 4 (x*sin(c8*t+c9))
- None have `v*sin(x)` or `v*sin(c*x+d)` as a term.

Candidate 65 has `c2*sin(c3*x + c4)` but this lacks the `v` multiplier. Setting c3=1, c4=0 gives `c2*sin(x)`, but the GT needs `v*sin(x)`, not just `sin(x)`.
